\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01705}01705\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\_RidgeGCV\`{}\ uses\ a\ Generalized\ Cross-\/Validation\ for\ model\ selection.\ It's\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01706}01706\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ efficient\ approximation\ of\ leave-\/one-\/out\ cross-\/validation\ (LOO-\/CV),\ where\ instead\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01707}01707\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ computing\ multiple\ models\ by\ excluding\ one\ data\ point\ at\ a\ time,\ it\ uses\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01708}01708\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ algebraic\ shortcut\ to\ approximate\ the\ LOO-\/CV\ error,\ making\ it\ faster\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01709}01709\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ computationally\ more\ efficient.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01710}01710\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01711}01711\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Using\ a\ naive\ grid-\/search\ approach\ with\ a\ leave-\/one-\/out\ cross-\/validation\ in\ contrast}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01712}01712\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ requires\ to\ fit\ \`{}n\_samples\`{}\ models\ to\ compute\ the\ prediction\ error\ for\ each\ sample}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01713}01713\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ and\ then\ to\ repeat\ this\ process\ for\ each\ alpha\ in\ the\ grid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01714}01714\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01715}01715\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Here,\ the\ prediction\ error\ for\ each\ sample\ is\ computed\ by\ solving\ a\ **single**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01716}01716\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ linear\ system\ (in\ other\ words\ a\ single\ model)\ via\ a\ matrix\ factorization\ (i.e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01717}01717\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ eigendecomposition\ or\ SVD)\ solving\ the\ problem\ stated\ in\ the\ Notes\ section.\ Finally,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__ridge_8py_source_l01718}01718\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ we\ need\ to\ repeat\ this\ process\ for\ each\ alpha\ in\ the\ grid.\ The\ detailed\ complexity}}
